msg:A very recommended hotel villa
In order to travel with the whole family, I searched for hotels in the suburbs of Beijing. Due to the epidemic, hotel prices have risen sharply, and I finally found this newly opened hotel to meet all needs. We are 2 adults, 1 teenager, 3 seniors.
The villa has a total of three floors. The 1st and 3rd floors have beds of 1.5 meters, and the second floor has 2 beds of 5+1.8 meters. Each floor has an independent toilet and shower, which solves the biggest problem. Close the door and do not interfere with each other.
Although the small living room on the first floor of the hotel is a little small, it is also pleasant. There is no problem eating fruit, chatting, or even playing poker.
Although the breakfast is not as good as a 5-star hotel, it is still rich, mainly Chinese food.
The hotel staff are very friendly. The hotel is located in the small town of Vernon. There is a small Monet garden (because there is a small lotus pond) and a few small animals. The children have no interest when they are older. You can enter from the parking lot. Call the hotel shuttle bus to and from, but in fact it is only a 5-minute walk.
All in all a good impression, should choose to come again.
